# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
find angle given three sides ^eklnUDrD

find side given other two and angle opp ^NE5YeTMH

every two sides with angle in between, just rotate the triangle ^8ZhmEJ7f

statinary points are points where the gradient is 0 so the first derivative has to be 0 ^Z6HVsqa1

to find the derivative of the inverse you first write the equation in function of x, find the derivative,
get the reciprocal (1/x), and finally replace the term if you can ^Aav06rrU
